        self._calibration_history: List[Dict] = []
        self._initialize_empirical_data()
    
    def _initialize_empirical_data(self):
        """初始化经验数据 - 基于行业通用值"""
        
        # 纸板：常见包装材料
        self._materials[MaterialType.CARDBOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CARDBOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.3, 1.5, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.08, 0.20, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(50, 200, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.0,  # 基准值
            compression_modulus=15.0   # 待校准
        )
        
        # 瓦楞纸：缓冲包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.CORRUGATED] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CORRUGATED,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(2.0, 8.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.15, 0.35, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(30, 120, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=0.7,
            compression_modulus=8.0
        )
        
        # 白卡纸：精品包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.2, 0.8, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.05, 0.15, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(80, 300, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.3,
            compression_modulus=25.0
        )
        
        # 灰板：精装书/礼盒
        self._materials[MaterialType.GREY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.GREY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(1.0, 3.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.20, 0.50, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(100, 400, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.5,
            compression_modulus=35.0
        )
        
        logger.info(f"材料数据库初始化完成: {len(self._materials)}种材料 (全部标记为待校准V)")
    
    def get_material(self, material_type: MaterialType) -> Optional[MaterialSpec]:
        return self._materials.get(material_type)
    
    def calibrate_from_validation(self, material_type: MaterialType, 
                                   validated_params: Dict[str, float],
                                   test_result: bool) -> bool:
        """
        从Playwright验证结果反校准参数
        V→F转化：验证通过后固化为已知
        """
        spec = self._materials.get(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return False
        
        # 记录校准历史
        calibration_record = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "material": material_type.value,
            "params": validated_params,
            "result": "PASS" if test_result else "FAIL"
        }
        self._calibration_history.append(calibration_record)
        
        if test_result:
            # 验证通过，收窄参数区间
            if "epsilon" in validated_params:
                eps = validated_params["epsilon"]
                # 贝叶斯更新：收窄区间
                spec.epsilon_range.min_val = max(spec.epsilon_range.min_val, eps * 0.8)
                spec.epsilon_range.max_val = min(spec.epsilon_range.max_val, eps * 1.2)
                spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            if "load" in validated_params:
                load = validated_params["load"]
                spec.load_capacity_range.min_val = max(spec.load_capacity_range.min_val, load * 0.9)
                spec.load_capacity_range.max_val = min(spec.load_capacity_range.max_val, load * 1.1)
                spec.load_capacity_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            logger.info(f"材料 {material_type.value} 参数校准完成")
        
        return True
    
    def export_calibration_report(self) -> Dict:
        """导出校准报告"""
        return {
            "materials": {k.value: v.to_dict() for k, v in self._materials.items()},
            "calibration_history": self._calibration_history[-10:],  # 最近10条
            "unresolved_v_count": sum(1 for v in self._materials.values() 
                                     if not v.epsilon_range.is_calibrated)
        }


# ============================================================================
# 第三部分：约束节点与链式传播引擎
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintNode:
    """
    约束节点 - F→V→F链式收敛的基本单元
    
    每个节点包含：
    - F: 固定约束（来自上游或物理定律）
    - V: 待求解变量
    - solve(): 求解V
    - validate(): 验证解是否满足约束
    """
    
    def __init__(self, level: ConstraintLevel, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        self.level = level
        self.material_db = material_db
        self.upstream_node: Optional[ConstraintNode] = None
        self.result: Optional[SolveResult] = None
        self._gate_threshold = 0.15  # 门控阈值 mm
    
    def set_upstream(self, node: ConstraintNode):
        """设置上游节点"""
        self.upstream_node = node
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """求解当前层级的V变量"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证解是否满足约束"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def propagate(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """
        链式传播：求解→验证→返回结果
        若无解，触发回溯或标记阻塞
        """
        # 1. 求解
        self.result = self.solve(input_data)
        
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.FAILED:
            # 2. 无解时尝试回溯
            if self.upstream_node and self._backtrack():
                # 回溯成功，重新求解
                self.result = self.solve(input_data)
            else:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.BLOCKED
                self.result.blocked_reason = "上游约束过紧，无法求解"
        
        # 3. 验证
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.SOLVED:
            is_valid, msg = self.validate(self.result.variables)
            if is_valid:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.VALIDATED
                self.result.confidence = self._calculate_confidence()
            else:
                self.result.error_message = msg
        
        return self.result
    
    def _backtrack(self) -> bool:
        """回溯：放宽上游约束"""
        if not self.upstream_node:
            return False
        
        # 尝试放宽门控阈值 10%
        self._gate_threshold *= 1.1
        logger.warning(f"回溯: 放宽 {self.level.value} 门控阈值至 {self._gate_threshold:.3f}")
        
        # 重新传播上游
        if self.upstream_node.result:
            self.upstream_node._gate_threshold *= 1.05
            return True
        return False
    
    def _calculate_confidence(self) -> float:
        """计算置信度"""
        base_confidence = 0.7
        
        # 材料参数已校准则提高置信度
        if self.level in [ConstraintLevel.V1_MATERIAL, ConstraintLevel.V3_PROCESS]:
            if self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD):
                spec = self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD)
                if spec and spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated:
                    base_confidence += 0.2
        
        return min(base_confidence, 1.0)


class F0_PhysicsNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    F₀ 物理约束层
    
    已知(F):
    - 切割力公式: F = P × L × K (压力×长度×系数)
    - 刀片几何参数
    - 物理定律不可违反
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(ConstraintLevel.F0_PHYSICS, material_db)
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        geometry: DieLineGeometry = input_data.get("geometry")
        material_type: MaterialType = input_data.get("material_type")
        
        if not geometry or not material_type:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message="缺少输入数据"
            )
        
        spec = self.material_db.get_material(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message=f"未知材料类型: {material_type}"
            )
        
        # 计算最小模切压力
        effective_length = geometry.effective_cutting_length() / 10  # cm
        min_pressure = (spec.load_capacity_range.min_val * effective_length * 
                       spec.cutting_force_factor)
        
        # 刀片厚度补偿 [BLOCKED: 使用经验值替代IADD数据]
        blade_compensation = self._get_blade_compensation(geometry.blade_thickness)
        
        return SolveResult(
            level=self.level,
            status=SolveStatus.SOLVED,
            variables={
                "min_cutting_pressure": min_pressure,
                "blade_compensation": blade_compensation,
                "effective_length_cm": effective_length
            },
            constraints={
                "total_length": geometry.total_length,
                "blade_thickness": geometry.blade_thickness,
                "material": material_type.value
            }
        )
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证物理约束"""
        min_pressure = solution.get("min_cutting_pressure", 0)
        if min_pressure <= 0:
            return False, "模切压力必须大于0"
        
        # 物理极限检查
        if min_pressure > 5000:  # 5000N 极限
            return False, f"模切压力 {min_pressure}N 超出设备极限"
        
        return True, ""
    
    def _get_blade_compensation(self, blade_thickness: float) -> float:
        """
        刀片厚度补偿算法
        
        [BLOCKED] 缺乏IADD官方规格数据
        临时方案：使用行业经验值
        - 0.45mm刀片 → 补偿0.15mm
        - 0.71mm刀片 → 补偿0.25mm
        """
        # 线性插值
        if blade_thickness <= 0.45:
            return 0.15
        elif blade_thickness >= 0.71:
            return 0.25
        else:
            return 0.15 + (blade_thickness - 0.45) / (0.71 - 0.45) * 0.10


class V1_MaterialNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    V₁ 材料变量层
    
    未知(V): 材料具体参数需要从经验数据库中选择
    策略：构建参数空间，通过约束传播收窄
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(Constraint

🛡️ 风险提示:
- [CD03] 内存泄漏: 循环引用/未释放资源/无限增长缓存
- [CD07] SQL注入/命令注入: 字符串拼接构建查询/命令

## 第 7 轮
📋 分析:
### 1. 问题要点拆解
- 构建约束传播求解器，实现7级链式收敛：F₀→V₁→F₁→V₂→F₂→V₃→F₃
- 每级F为固定约束，V为待求解变量
- 关联ULDS多层级（L1数学/L2物理/L3化学/L6系统/L8工程）
- 需与Playwright自动验证闭环对接

### 2. 关键概念识别
- **约束传播**：上游F确定后，V的解空间收窄，再固化为下游F
- **链式收敛**：误差逐级传递并累积，需每级设门控阈值
- **材料-结构-工艺耦合**：V₁材料选择直接影响V₂结构设计和V₃工艺参数

### 3. 初步分析结论

**已知(F)梳理：**
| 层级 | 已知固定约束 | 来源 |
|------|-------------|------|
| F₀ | 模切物理定律(切割力=压力×刀线长度)、刀片几何参数 | L2物理 |
| F₁ | 误差不能超过±0.15mm(行业通用公差)、累积误差公式 | L8工程 |
| F₂ | 荷载计算公式(集中力/均布力)、瓦楞纸抗压公式 | L1+L2 |
| F₃ | 质量验收标准(尺寸偏差/压痕深度/切断率) | 行业标准 |
| 代码 | deduction_runner.py推演引擎框架、DB表结构 | 已有基座 |

**未知(V)识别：**
| 变量 | 探索空间 | 不确定度 |
|------|---------|---------|
| V₁ | 纸板/瓦楞/白卡/灰板各自[εmin,εmax]和[Fmin,Fmax] | 高 |
| V₂ | 桥接结构/过桥尺寸/刀线布局的参数化表达 | 中 |
| V₃ | 模切压力、刀片类型选择、压痕线宽深比 | 中 |
| 隐含V | 各级F→V→V→F之间的耦合系数/传递函数 | 高 |

### 4. 双轨推演策略

**对已知——最短路径：**
- 

💻 代码:
# F→V→F 约束传播求解器实现

基于"知与不知"元框架，我将实现7级链式收敛的约束传播求解器。

## 分析结论

**已知(F)**：物理定律、质量标准、已有代码框架
**未知(V)**：材料参数区间、耦合传递函数、工艺参数

**策略**：对已知直接编码，对未知构建自解框架+Playwright验证闭环

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
F→V→F 约束传播求解器 - 刀模设计项目 [p_diepre]
实现7级链式收敛：F₀(物理)→V₁(材料)→F₁(误差范围)→V₂(结构)→F₂(荷载)→V₃(工艺)→F₃(质量)

基于"知与不知"元框架：
- 已知(F): 物理定律、质量标准、已有代码 → 最短路径编码
- 未知(V): 材料参数、耦合系数 → 见路不走，构建自解框架
"""

from __future__ import annotations
import json
import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Optional, Dict, List, Tuple, Any, Callable
from enum import Enum
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
import logging

# 配置日志
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# ============================================================================
# 第一部分：数据结构定义 (已知F的固化)
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintLevel(Enum):
    """约束层级枚举 - ULDS映射"""
    F0_PHYSICS = "F₀物理"      # L2物理：切割力公式、刀片几何
    V1_MATERIAL = "V₁材料"     # L3化学：材料特性参数
    F1_TOLERANCE = "F₁误差"    # L8工程：公差范围、累积误差
    V2_STRUCTURE = "V₂结构"    # L1数学：桥接尺寸、刀线布局
    F2_LOAD = "F₂荷载"         # L2物理：抗压公式、力分布
    V3_PROCESS = "V₃工艺"      # L6系统：模切压力、压痕参数
    F3_QUALITY = "F₃质量"      # L8工程：验收标准


class MaterialType(Enum):
    """材料类型"""
    CARDBOARD = "纸板"
    CORRUGATED = "瓦楞"
    IVORY_BOARD = "白卡"
    GREY_BOARD = "灰板"


class SolveStatus(Enum):
    """求解状态"""
    PENDING = "待求解"
    SOLVED = "已求解"
    VALIDATED = "已验证"
    FAILED = "无解"
    BLOCKED = "阻塞"


@dataclass
class ValueRange:
    """值范围表示 [min, max]"""
    min_val: float
    max_val: float
    unit: str = ""
    is_calibrated: bool = False  # V标记：是否已校准
    
    def contains(self, value: float) -> bool:
        return self.min_val <= value <= self.max_val
    
    def midpoint(self) -> float:
        return (self.min_val + self.max_val) / 2
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "min": self.min_val,
            "max": self.max_val,
            "unit": self.unit,
            "calibrated": self.is_calibrated
        }


@dataclass
class MaterialSpec:
    """材料规格 - V₁变量空间"""
    material_type: MaterialType
    thickness_range: ValueRange      # 厚度范围 mm
    epsilon_range: ValueRange        # 误差范围 mm
    load_capacity_range: ValueRange  # 承载范围 N/cm
    cutting_force_factor: float      # 切割力系数 (V标记: 待校准)
    compression_modulus: float       # 抗压模量 MPa (V标记: 待校准)
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "type": self.material_type.value,
            "thickness": self.thickness_range.to_dict(),
            "epsilon": self.epsilon_range.to_dict(),
            "load_capacity": self.load_capacity_range.to_dict(),
            "cutting_force_factor": self.cutting_force_factor,
            "compression_modulus": self.compression_modulus
        }


@dataclass 
class DieLineGeometry:
    """刀线几何参数"""
    total_length: float      # 总刀线长度 mm
    bridge_count: int        # 过桥数量
    bridge_width: float      # 过桥宽度 mm (标准3-5mm)
    blade_thickness: float   # 刀片厚度 mm [BLOCKED: 缺乏IADD官方数据，使用经验值0.45/0.71]
    blade_height: float      # 刀片高度 mm (标准23.8mm)
    
    def effective_cutting_length(self) -> float:
        """有效切割长度 = 总长度 - 过桥总宽度"""
        return self.total_length - (self.bridge_count * self.bridge_width)


@dataclass
class SolveResult:
    """求解结果"""
    level: ConstraintLevel
    status: SolveStatus
    variables: Dict[str, Any]           # 求解得到的变量
    constraints: Dict[str, Any]         # 固化的约束
    confidence: float = 0.0             # 置信度 0-1
    error_message: str = ""
    blocked_reason: str = ""


# ============================================================================
# 第二部分：材料经验数据库 (V₁未知→构建自解框架)
# ============================================================================

class MaterialDatabase:
    """
    材料特性数据库
    
    策略：见路不走 - 不依赖IADD官方数据(已阻塞)
    采用反向工程法：从已有刀模图成品反推参数区间
    所有值标记为V(待校准)，通过Playwright验证闭环逐步固化为F
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self._materials: Dict[MaterialType, MaterialSpec] = {}
        self._calibration_history: List[Dict] = []
        self._initialize_empirical_data()
    
    def _initialize_empirical_data(self):
        """初始化经验数据 - 基于行业通用值"""
        
        # 纸板：常见包装材料
        self._materials[MaterialType.CARDBOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CARDBOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.3, 1.5, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.08, 0.20, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(50, 200, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.0,  # 基准值
            compression_modulus=15.0   # 待校准
        )
        
        # 瓦楞纸：缓冲包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.CORRUGATED] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CORRUGATED,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(2.0, 8.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.15, 0.35, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(30, 120, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=0.7,
            compression_modulus=8.0
        )
        
        # 白卡纸：精品包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.2, 0.8, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.05, 0.15, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(80, 300, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.3,
            compression_modulus=25.0
        )
        
        # 灰板：精装书/礼盒
        self._materials[MaterialType.GREY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.GREY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(1.0, 3.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.20, 0.50, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(100, 400, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.5,
            compression_modulus=35.0
        )
        
        logger.info(f"材料数据库初始化完成: {len(self._materials)}种材料 (全部标记为待校准V)")
    
    def get_material(self, material_type: MaterialType) -> Optional[MaterialSpec]:
        return self._materials.get(material_type)
    
    def calibrate_from_validation(self, material_type: MaterialType, 
                                   validated_params: Dict[str, float],
                                   test_result: bool) -> bool:
        """
        从Playwright验证结果反校准参数
        V→F转化：验证通过后固化为已知
        """
        spec = self._materials.get(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return False
        
        # 记录校准历史
        calibration_record = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "material": material_type.value,
            "params": validated_params,
            "result": "PASS" if test_result else "FAIL"
        }
        self._calibration_history.append(calibration_record)
        
        if test_result:
            # 验证通过，收窄参数区间
            if "epsilon" in validated_params:
                eps = validated_params["epsilon"]
                # 贝叶斯更新：收窄区间
                spec.epsilon_range.min_val = max(spec.epsilon_range.min_val, eps * 0.8)
                spec.epsilon_range.max_val = min(spec.epsilon_range.max_val, eps * 1.2)
                spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            if "load" in validated_params:
                load = validated_params["load"]
                spec.load_capacity_range.min_val = max(spec.load_capacity_range.min_val, load * 0.9)
                spec.load_capacity_range.max_val = min(spec.load_capacity_range.max_val, load * 1.1)
                spec.load_capacity_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            logger.info(f"材料 {material_type.value} 参数校准完成")
        
        return True
    
    def export_calibration_report(self) -> Dict:
        """导出校准报告"""
        return {
            "materials": {k.value: v.to_dict() for k, v in self._materials.items()},
            "calibration_history": self._calibration_history[-10:],  # 最近10条
            "unresolved_v_count": sum(1 for v in self._materials.values() 
                                     if not v.epsilon_range.is_calibrated)
        }


# ============================================================================
# 第三部分：约束节点与链式传播引擎
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintNode:
    """
    约束节点 - F→V→F链式收敛的基本单元
    
    每个节点包含：
    - F: 固定约束（来自上游或物理定律）
    - V: 待求解变量
    - solve(): 求解V
    - validate(): 验证解是否满足约束
    """
    
    def __init__(self, level: ConstraintLevel, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        self.level = level
        self.material_db = material_db
        self.upstream_node: Optional[ConstraintNode] = None
        self.result: Optional[SolveResult] = None
        self._gate_threshold = 0.15  # 门控阈值 mm
    
    def set_upstream(self, node: ConstraintNode):
        """设置上游节点"""
        self.upstream_node = node
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """求解当前层级的V变量"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证解是否满足约束"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def propagate(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """
        链式传播：求解→验证→返回结果
        若无解，触发回溯或标记阻塞
        """
        # 1. 求解
        self.result = self.solve(input_data)
        
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.FAILED:
            # 2. 无解时尝试回溯
            if self.upstream_node and self._backtrack():
                # 回溯成功，重新求解
                self.result = self.solve(input_data)
            else:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.BLOCKED
                self.result.blocked_reason = "上游约束过紧，无法求解"
        
        # 3. 验证
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.SOLVED:
            is_valid, msg = self.validate(self.result.variables)
            if is_valid:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.VALIDATED
                self.result.confidence = self._calculate_confidence()
            else:
                self.result.error_message = msg
        
        return self.result
    
    def _backtrack(self) -> bool:
        """回溯：放宽上游约束"""
        if not self.upstream_node:
            return False
        
        # 尝试放宽门控阈值 10%
        self._gate_threshold *= 1.1
        logger.warning(f"回溯: 放宽 {self.level.value} 门控阈值至 {self._gate_threshold:.3f}")
        
        # 重新传播上游
        if self.upstream_node.result:
            self.upstream_node._gate_threshold *= 1.05
            return True
        return False
    
    def _calculate_confidence(self) -> float:
        """计算置信度"""
        base_confidence = 0.7
        
        # 材料参数已校准则提高置信度
        if self.level in [ConstraintLevel.V1_MATERIAL, ConstraintLevel.V3_PROCESS]:
            if self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD):
                spec = self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD)
                if spec and spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated:
                    base_confidence += 0.2
        
        return min(base_confidence, 1.0)


class F0_PhysicsNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    F₀ 物理约束层
    
    已知(F):
    - 切割力公式: F = P × L × K (压力×长度×系数)
    - 刀片几何参数
    - 物理定律不可违反
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(ConstraintLevel.F0_PHYSICS, material_db)
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        geometry: DieLineGeometry = input_data.get("geometry")
        material_type: MaterialType = input_data.get("material_type")
        
        if not geometry or not material_type:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message="缺少输入数据"
            )
        
        spec = self.material_db.get_material(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message=f"未知材料类型: {material_type}"
            )
        
        # 计算最小模切压力
        effective_length = geometry.effective_cutting_length() / 10  # cm
        min_pressure = (spec.load_capacity_range.min_val * effective_length * 
                       spec.cutting_force_factor)
        
        # 刀片厚度补偿 [BLOCKED: 使用经验值替代IADD数据]
        blade_compensation = self._get_blade_compensation(geometry.blade_thickness)
        
        return SolveResult(
            level=self.level,
            status=SolveStatus.SOLVED,
            variables={
                "min_cutting_pressure": min_pressure,
                "blade_compensation": blade_compensation,
                "effective_length_cm": effective_length
            },
            constraints={
                "total_length": geometry.total_length,
                "blade_thickness": geometry.blade_thickness,
                "material": material_type.value
            }
        )
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证物理约束"""
        min_pressure = solution.get("min_cutting_pressure", 0)
        if min_pressure <= 0:
            return False, "模切压力必须大于0"
        
        # 物理极限检查
        if min_pressure > 5000:  # 5000N 极限
            return False, f"模切压力 {min_pressure}N 超出设备极限"
        
        return True, ""
    
    def _get_blade_compensation(self, blade_thickness: float) -> float:
        """
        刀片厚度补偿算法
        
        [BLOCKED] 缺乏IADD官方规格数据
        临时方案：使用行业经验值
        - 0.45mm刀片 → 补偿0.15mm
        - 0.71mm刀片 → 补偿0.25mm
        """
        # 线性插值
        if blade_thickness <= 0.45:
            return 0.15
        elif blade_thickness >= 0.71:
            return 0.25
        else:
            return 0.15 + (blade_thickness - 0.45) / (0.71 - 0.45) * 0.10


class V1_MaterialNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    V₁ 材料变量层
    
    未知(V): 材料具体参数需要从经验数据库中选择
    策略：构建参数空间，通过约束传播收窄
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(Constraint

🛡️ 风险提示:
- [CD03] 内存泄漏: 循环引用/未释放资源/无限增长缓存
- [CD07] SQL注入/命令注入: 字符串拼接构建查询/命令

## 第 8 轮
📋 分析:
### 1. 问题要点拆解
- 构建约束传播求解器，实现7级链式收敛：F₀→V₁→F₁→V₂→F₂→V₃→F₃
- 每级F为固定约束，V为待求解变量
- 关联ULDS多层级（L1数学/L2物理/L3化学/L6系统/L8工程）
- 需与Playwright自动验证闭环对接

### 2. 关键概念识别
- **约束传播**：上游F确定后，V的解空间收窄，再固化为下游F
- **链式收敛**：误差逐级传递并累积，需每级设门控阈值
- **材料-结构-工艺耦合**：V₁材料选择直接影响V₂结构设计和V₃工艺参数

### 3. 初步分析结论

**已知(F)梳理：**
| 层级 | 已知固定约束 | 来源 |
|------|-------------|------|
| F₀ | 模切物理定律(切割力=压力×刀线长度)、刀片几何参数 | L2物理 |
| F₁ | 误差不能超过±0.15mm(行业通用公差)、累积误差公式 | L8工程 |
| F₂ | 荷载计算公式(集中力/均布力)、瓦楞纸抗压公式 | L1+L2 |
| F₃ | 质量验收标准(尺寸偏差/压痕深度/切断率) | 行业标准 |
| 代码 | deduction_runner.py推演引擎框架、DB表结构 | 已有基座 |

**未知(V)识别：**
| 变量 | 探索空间 | 不确定度 |
|------|---------|---------|
| V₁ | 纸板/瓦楞/白卡/灰板各自[εmin,εmax]和[Fmin,Fmax] | 高 |
| V₂ | 桥接结构/过桥尺寸/刀线布局的参数化表达 | 中 |
| V₃ | 模切压力、刀片类型选择、压痕线宽深比 | 中 |
| 隐含V | 各级F→V→V→F之间的耦合系数/传递函数 | 高 |

### 4. 双轨推演策略

**对已知——最短路径：**
- 

💻 代码:
# F→V→F 约束传播求解器实现

基于"知与不知"元框架，我将实现7级链式收敛的约束传播求解器。

## 分析结论

**已知(F)**：物理定律、质量标准、已有代码框架
**未知(V)**：材料参数区间、耦合传递函数、工艺参数

**策略**：对已知直接编码，对未知构建自解框架+Playwright验证闭环

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
F→V→F 约束传播求解器 - 刀模设计项目 [p_diepre]
实现7级链式收敛：F₀(物理)→V₁(材料)→F₁(误差范围)→V₂(结构)→F₂(荷载)→V₃(工艺)→F₃(质量)

基于"知与不知"元框架：
- 已知(F): 物理定律、质量标准、已有代码 → 最短路径编码
- 未知(V): 材料参数、耦合系数 → 见路不走，构建自解框架
"""

from __future__ import annotations
import json
import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Optional, Dict, List, Tuple, Any, Callable
from enum import Enum
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
import logging

# 配置日志
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# ============================================================================
# 第一部分：数据结构定义 (已知F的固化)
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintLevel(Enum):
    """约束层级枚举 - ULDS映射"""
    F0_PHYSICS = "F₀物理"      # L2物理：切割力公式、刀片几何
    V1_MATERIAL = "V₁材料"     # L3化学：材料特性参数
    F1_TOLERANCE = "F₁误差"    # L8工程：公差范围、累积误差
    V2_STRUCTURE = "V₂结构"    # L1数学：桥接尺寸、刀线布局
    F2_LOAD = "F₂荷载"         # L2物理：抗压公式、力分布
    V3_PROCESS = "V₃工艺"      # L6系统：模切压力、压痕参数
    F3_QUALITY = "F₃质量"      # L8工程：验收标准


class MaterialType(Enum):
    """材料类型"""
    CARDBOARD = "纸板"
    CORRUGATED = "瓦楞"
    IVORY_BOARD = "白卡"
    GREY_BOARD = "灰板"


class SolveStatus(Enum):
    """求解状态"""
    PENDING = "待求解"
    SOLVED = "已求解"
    VALIDATED = "已验证"
    FAILED = "无解"
    BLOCKED = "阻塞"


@dataclass
class ValueRange:
    """值范围表示 [min, max]"""
    min_val: float
    max_val: float
    unit: str = ""
    is_calibrated: bool = False  # V标记：是否已校准
    
    def contains(self, value: float) -> bool:
        return self.min_val <= value <= self.max_val
    
    def midpoint(self) -> float:
        return (self.min_val + self.max_val) / 2
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "min": self.min_val,
            "max": self.max_val,
            "unit": self.unit,
            "calibrated": self.is_calibrated
        }


@dataclass
class MaterialSpec:
    """材料规格 - V₁变量空间"""
    material_type: MaterialType
    thickness_range: ValueRange      # 厚度范围 mm
    epsilon_range: ValueRange        # 误差范围 mm
    load_capacity_range: ValueRange  # 承载范围 N/cm
    cutting_force_factor: float      # 切割力系数 (V标记: 待校准)
    compression_modulus: float       # 抗压模量 MPa (V标记: 待校准)
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "type": self.material_type.value,
            "thickness": self.thickness_range.to_dict(),
            "epsilon": self.epsilon_range.to_dict(),
            "load_capacity": self.load_capacity_range.to_dict(),
            "cutting_force_factor": self.cutting_force_factor,
            "compression_modulus": self.compression_modulus
        }


@dataclass 
class DieLineGeometry:
    """刀线几何参数"""
    total_length: float      # 总刀线长度 mm
    bridge_count: int        # 过桥数量
    bridge_width: float      # 过桥宽度 mm (标准3-5mm)
    blade_thickness: float   # 刀片厚度 mm [BLOCKED: 缺乏IADD官方数据，使用经验值0.45/0.71]
    blade_height: float      # 刀片高度 mm (标准23.8mm)
    
    def effective_cutting_length(self) -> float:
        """有效切割长度 = 总长度 - 过桥总宽度"""
        return self.total_length - (self.bridge_count * self.bridge_width)


@dataclass
class SolveResult:
    """求解结果"""
    level: ConstraintLevel
    status: SolveStatus
    variables: Dict[str, Any]           # 求解得到的变量
    constraints: Dict[str, Any]         # 固化的约束
    confidence: float = 0.0             # 置信度 0-1
    error_message: str = ""
    blocked_reason: str = ""


# ============================================================================
# 第二部分：材料经验数据库 (V₁未知→构建自解框架)
# ============================================================================

class MaterialDatabase:
    """
    材料特性数据库
    
    策略：见路不走 - 不依赖IADD官方数据(已阻塞)
    采用反向工程法：从已有刀模图成品反推参数区间
    所有值标记为V(待校准)，通过Playwright验证闭环逐步固化为F
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self._materials: Dict[MaterialType, MaterialSpec] = {}
        self._calibration_history: List[Dict] = []
        self._initialize_empirical_data()
    
    def _initialize_empirical_data(self):
        """初始化经验数据 - 基于行业通用值"""
        
        # 纸板：常见包装材料
        self._materials[MaterialType.CARDBOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CARDBOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.3, 1.5, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.08, 0.20, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(50, 200, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.0,  # 基准值
            compression_modulus=15.0   # 待校准
        )
        
        # 瓦楞纸：缓冲包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.CORRUGATED] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CORRUGATED,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(2.0, 8.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.15, 0.35, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(30, 120, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=0.7,
            compression_modulus=8.0
        )
        
        # 白卡纸：精品包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.2, 0.8, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.05, 0.15, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(80, 300, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.3,
            compression_modulus=25.0
        )
        
        # 灰板：精装书/礼盒
        self._materials[MaterialType.GREY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.GREY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(1.0, 3.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.20, 0.50, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(100, 400, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.5,
            compression_modulus=35.0
        )
        
        logger.info(f"材料数据库初始化完成: {len(self._materials)}种材料 (全部标记为待校准V)")
    
    def get_material(self, material_type: MaterialType) -> Optional[MaterialSpec]:
        return self._materials.get(material_type)
    
    def calibrate_from_validation(self, material_type: MaterialType, 
                                   validated_params: Dict[str, float],
                                   test_result: bool) -> bool:
        """
        从Playwright验证结果反校准参数
        V→F转化：验证通过后固化为已知
        """
        spec = self._materials.get(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return False
        
        # 记录校准历史
        calibration_record = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "material": material_type.value,
            "params": validated_params,
            "result": "PASS" if test_result else "FAIL"
        }
        self._calibration_history.append(calibration_record)
        
        if test_result:
            # 验证通过，收窄参数区间
            if "epsilon" in validated_params:
                eps = validated_params["epsilon"]
                # 贝叶斯更新：收窄区间
                spec.epsilon_range.min_val = max(spec.epsilon_range.min_val, eps * 0.8)
                spec.epsilon_range.max_val = min(spec.epsilon_range.max_val, eps * 1.2)
                spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            if "load" in validated_params:
                load = validated_params["load"]
                spec.load_capacity_range.min_val = max(spec.load_capacity_range.min_val, load * 0.9)
                spec.load_capacity_range.max_val = min(spec.load_capacity_range.max_val, load * 1.1)
                spec.load_capacity_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            logger.info(f"材料 {material_type.value} 参数校准完成")
        
        return True
    
    def export_calibration_report(self) -> Dict:
        """导出校准报告"""
        return {
            "materials": {k.value: v.to_dict() for k, v in self._materials.items()},
            "calibration_history": self._calibration_history[-10:],  # 最近10条
            "unresolved_v_count": sum(1 for v in self._materials.values() 
                                     if not v.epsilon_range.is_calibrated)
        }


# ============================================================================
# 第三部分：约束节点与链式传播引擎
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintNode:
    """
    约束节点 - F→V→F链式收敛的基本单元
    
    每个节点包含：
    - F: 固定约束（来自上游或物理定律）
    - V: 待求解变量
    - solve(): 求解V
    - validate(): 验证解是否满足约束
    """
    
    def __init__(self, level: ConstraintLevel, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        self.level = level
        self.material_db = material_db
        self.upstream_node: Optional[ConstraintNode] = None
        self.result: Optional[SolveResult] = None
        self._gate_threshold = 0.15  # 门控阈值 mm
    
    def set_upstream(self, node: ConstraintNode):
        """设置上游节点"""
        self.upstream_node = node
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """求解当前层级的V变量"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证解是否满足约束"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def propagate(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """
        链式传播：求解→验证→返回结果
        若无解，触发回溯或标记阻塞
        """
        # 1. 求解
        self.result = self.solve(input_data)
        
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.FAILED:
            # 2. 无解时尝试回溯
            if self.upstream_node and self._backtrack():
                # 回溯成功，重新求解
                self.result = self.solve(input_data)
            else:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.BLOCKED
                self.result.blocked_reason = "上游约束过紧，无法求解"
        
        # 3. 验证
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.SOLVED:
            is_valid, msg = self.validate(self.result.variables)
            if is_valid:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.VALIDATED
                self.result.confidence = self._calculate_confidence()
            else:
                self.result.error_message = msg
        
        return self.result
    
    def _backtrack(self) -> bool:
        """回溯：放宽上游约束"""
        if not self.upstream_node:
            return False
        
        # 尝试放宽门控阈值 10%
        self._gate_threshold *= 1.1
        logger.warning(f"回溯: 放宽 {self.level.value} 门控阈值至 {self._gate_threshold:.3f}")
        
        # 重新传播上游
        if self.upstream_node.result:
            self.upstream_node._gate_threshold *= 1.05
            return True
        return False
    
    def _calculate_confidence(self) -> float:
        """计算置信度"""
        base_confidence = 0.7
        
        # 材料参数已校准则提高置信度
        if self.level in [ConstraintLevel.V1_MATERIAL, ConstraintLevel.V3_PROCESS]:
            if self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD):
                spec = self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD)
                if spec and spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated:
                    base_confidence += 0.2
        
        return min(base_confidence, 1.0)


class F0_PhysicsNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    F₀ 物理约束层
    
    已知(F):
    - 切割力公式: F = P × L × K (压力×长度×系数)
    - 刀片几何参数
    - 物理定律不可违反
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(ConstraintLevel.F0_PHYSICS, material_db)
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        geometry: DieLineGeometry = input_data.get("geometry")
        material_type: MaterialType = input_data.get("material_type")
        
        if not geometry or not material_type:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message="缺少输入数据"
            )
        
        spec = self.material_db.get_material(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message=f"未知材料类型: {material_type}"
            )
        
        # 计算最小模切压力
        effective_length = geometry.effective_cutting_length() / 10  # cm
        min_pressure = (spec.load_capacity_range.min_val * effective_length * 
                       spec.cutting_force_factor)
        
        # 刀片厚度补偿 [BLOCKED: 使用经验值替代IADD数据]
        blade_compensation = self._get_blade_compensation(geometry.blade_thickness)
        
        return SolveResult(
            level=self.level,
            status=SolveStatus.SOLVED,
            variables={
                "min_cutting_pressure": min_pressure,
                "blade_compensation": blade_compensation,
                "effective_length_cm": effective_length
            },
            constraints={
                "total_length": geometry.total_length,
                "blade_thickness": geometry.blade_thickness,
                "material": material_type.value
            }
        )
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证物理约束"""
        min_pressure = solution.get("min_cutting_pressure", 0)
        if min_pressure <= 0:
            return False, "模切压力必须大于0"
        
        # 物理极限检查
        if min_pressure > 5000:  # 5000N 极限
            return False, f"模切压力 {min_pressure}N 超出设备极限"
        
        return True, ""
    
    def _get_blade_compensation(self, blade_thickness: float) -> float:
        """
        刀片厚度补偿算法
        
        [BLOCKED] 缺乏IADD官方规格数据
        临时方案：使用行业经验值
        - 0.45mm刀片 → 补偿0.15mm
        - 0.71mm刀片 → 补偿0.25mm
        """
        # 线性插值
        if blade_thickness <= 0.45:
            return 0.15
        elif blade_thickness >= 0.71:
            return 0.25
        else:
            return 0.15 + (blade_thickness - 0.45) / (0.71 - 0.45) * 0.10


class V1_MaterialNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    V₁ 材料变量层
    
    未知(V): 材料具体参数需要从经验数据库中选择
    策略：构建参数空间，通过约束传播收窄
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(Constraint

| 隐含V | 各级F→V→V→F之间的耦合系数/传递函数 | 高 |

# F→V→F 约束传播求解器实现

基于"知与不知"元框架，我将实现7级链式收敛的约束传播求解器。

## 分析结论

**已知(F)**：物理定律、质量标准、已有代码框架
**未知(V)**：材料参数区间、耦合传递函数、工艺参数

**策略**：对已知直接编码，对未知构建自解框架+Playwright验证闭环

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
F→V→F 约束传播求解器 - 刀模设计项目 [p_diepre]
实现7级链式收敛：F₀(物理)→V₁(材料)→F₁(误差范围)→V₂(结构)→F₂(荷载)→V₃(工艺)→F₃(质量)

基于"知与不知"元框架：
- 已知(F): 物理定律、质量标准、已有代码 → 最短路径编码
- 未知(V): 材料参数、耦合系数 → 见路不走，构建自解框架
"""

from __future__ import annotations
import json
import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Optional, Dict, List, Tuple, Any, Callable
from enum import Enum
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
import logging

# 配置日志
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# ============================================================================
# 第一部分：数据结构定义 (已知F的固化)
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintLevel(Enum):
    """约束层级枚举 - ULDS映射"""
    F0_PHYSICS = "F₀物理"      # L2物理：切割力公式、刀片几何
    V1_MATERIAL = "V₁材料"     # L3化学：材料特性参数
    F1_TOLERANCE = "F₁误差"    # L8工程：公差范围、累积误差
    V2_STRUCTURE = "V₂结构"    # L1数学：桥接尺寸、刀线布局
    F2_LOAD = "F₂荷载"         # L2物理：抗压公式、力分布
    V3_PROCESS = "V₃工艺"      # L6系统：模切压力、压痕参数
    F3_QUALITY = "F₃质量"      # L8工程：验收标准


class MaterialType(Enum):
    """材料类型"""
    CARDBOARD = "纸板"
    CORRUGATED = "瓦楞"
    IVORY_BOARD = "白卡"
    GREY_BOARD = "灰板"


class SolveStatus(Enum):
    """求解状态"""
    PENDING = "待求解"
    SOLVED = "已求解"
    VALIDATED = "已验证"
    FAILED = "无解"
    BLOCKED = "阻塞"


@dataclass
class ValueRange:
    """值范围表示 [min, max]"""
    min_val: float
    max_val: float
    unit: str = ""
    is_calibrated: bool = False  # V标记：是否已校准
    
    def contains(self, value: float) -> bool:
        return self.min_val <= value <= self.max_val
    
    def midpoint(self) -> float:
        return (self.min_val + self.max_val) / 2
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "min": self.min_val,
            "max": self.max_val,
            "unit": self.unit,
            "calibrated": self.is_calibrated
        }


@dataclass
class MaterialSpec:
    """材料规格 - V₁变量空间"""
    material_type: MaterialType
    thickness_range: ValueRange      # 厚度范围 mm
    epsilon_range: ValueRange        # 误差范围 mm
    load_capacity_range: ValueRange  # 承载范围 N/cm
    cutting_force_factor: float      # 切割力系数 (V标记: 待校准)
    compression_modulus: float       # 抗压模量 MPa (V标记: 待校准)
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "type": self.material_type.value,
            "thickness": self.thickness_range.to_dict(),
            "epsilon": self.epsilon_range.to_dict(),
            "load_capacity": self.load_capacity_range.to_dict(),
            "cutting_force_factor": self.cutting_force_factor,
            "compression_modulus": self.compression_modulus
        }


@dataclass 
class DieLineGeometry:
    """刀线几何参数"""
    total_length: float      # 总刀线长度 mm
    bridge_count: int        # 过桥数量
    bridge_width: float      # 过桥宽度 mm (标准3-5mm)
    blade_thickness: float   # 刀片厚度 mm [BLOCKED: 缺乏IADD官方数据，使用经验值0.45/0.71]
    blade_height: float      # 刀片高度 mm (标准23.8mm)
    
    def effective_cutting_length(self) -> float:
        """有效切割长度 = 总长度 - 过桥总宽度"""
        return self.total_length - (self.bridge_count * self.bridge_width)


@dataclass
class SolveResult:
    """求解结果"""
    level: ConstraintLevel
    status: SolveStatus
    variables: Dict[str, Any]           # 求解得到的变量
    constraints: Dict[str, Any]         # 固化的约束
    confidence: float = 0.0             # 置信度 0-1
    error_message: str = ""
    blocked_reason: str = ""


# ============================================================================
# 第二部分：材料经验数据库 (V₁未知→构建自解框架)
# ============================================================================

class MaterialDatabase:
    """
    材料特性数据库
    
    策略：见路不走 - 不依赖IADD官方数据(已阻塞)
    采用反向工程法：从已有刀模图成品反推参数区间
    所有值标记为V(待校准)，通过Playwright验证闭环逐步固化为F
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self._materials: Dict[MaterialType, MaterialSpec] = {}
        self._calibration_history: List[Dict] = []
        self._initialize_empirical_data()
    
    def _initialize_empirical_data(self):
        """初始化经验数据 - 基于行业通用值"""
        
        # 纸板：常见包装材料
        self._materials[MaterialType.CARDBOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CARDBOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.3, 1.5, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.08, 0.20, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(50, 200, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.0,  # 基准值
            compression_modulus=15.0   # 待校准
        )
        
        # 瓦楞纸：缓冲包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.CORRUGATED] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CORRUGATED,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(2.0, 8.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.15, 0.35, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(30, 120, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=0.7,
            compression_modulus=8.0
        )
        
        # 白卡纸：精品包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.2, 0.8, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.05, 0.15, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(80, 300, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.3,
            compression_modulus=25.0
        )
        
        # 灰板：精装书/礼盒
        self._materials[MaterialType.GREY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.GREY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(1.0, 3.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.20, 0.50, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(100, 400, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.5,
            compression_modulus=35.0
        )
        
        logger.info(f"材料数据库初始化完成: {len(self._materials)}种材料 (全部标记为待校准V)")
    
    def get_material(self, material_type: MaterialType) -> Optional[MaterialSpec]:
        return self._materials.get(material_type)
    
    def calibrate_from_validation(self, material_type: MaterialType, 
                                   validated_params: Dict[str, float],
                                   test_result: bool) -> bool:
        """
        从Playwright验证结果反校准参数
        V→F转化：验证通过后固化为已知
        """
        spec = self._materials.get(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return False
        
        # 记录校准历史
        calibration_record = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "material": material_type.value,
            "params": validated_params,
            "result": "PASS" if test_result else "FAIL"
        }
        self._calibration_history.append(calibration_record)
        
        if test_result:
            # 验证通过，收窄参数区间
            if "epsilon" in validated_params:
                eps = validated_params["epsilon"]
                # 贝叶斯更新：收窄区间
                spec.epsilon_range.min_val = max(spec.epsilon_range.min_val, eps * 0.8)
                spec.epsilon_range.max_val = min(spec.epsilon_range.max_val, eps * 1.2)
                spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            if "load" in validated_params:
                load = validated_params["load"]
                spec.load_capacity_range.min_val = max(spec.load_capacity_range.min_val, load * 0.9)
                spec.load_capacity_range.max_val = min(spec.load_capacity_range.max_val, load * 1.1)
                spec.load_capacity_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            logger.info(f"材料 {material_type.value} 参数校准完成")
        
        return True
    
    def export_calibration_report(self) -> Dict:
        """导出校准报告"""
        return {
            "materials": {k.value: v.to_dict() for k, v in self._materials.items()},
            "calibration_history": self._calibration_history[-10:],  # 最近10条
            "unresolved_v_count": sum(1 for v in self._materials.values() 
                                     if not v.epsilon_range.is_calibrated)
        }


# ============================================================================
# 第三部分：约束节点与链式传播引擎
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintNode:
    """
    约束节点 - F→V→F链式收敛的基本单元
    
    每个节点包含：
    - F: 固定约束（来自上游或物理定律）
    - V: 待求解变量
    - solve(): 求解V
    - validate(): 验证解是否满足约束
    """
    
    def __init__(self, level: ConstraintLevel, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        self.level = level
        self.material_db = material_db
        self.upstream_node: Optional[ConstraintNode] = None
        self.result: Optional[SolveResult] = None
        self._gate_threshold = 0.15  # 门控阈值 mm
    
    def set_upstream(self, node: ConstraintNode):
        """设置上游节点"""
        self.upstream_node = node
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """求解当前层级的V变量"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证解是否满足约束"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def propagate(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """
        链式传播：求解→验证→返回结果
        若无解，触发回溯或标记阻塞
        """
        # 1. 求解
        self.result = self.solve(input_data)
        
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.FAILED:
            # 2. 无解时尝试回溯
            if self.upstream_node and self._backtrack():
                # 回溯成功，重新求解
                self.result = self.solve(input_data)
            else:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.BLOCKED
                self.result.blocked_reason = "上游约束过紧，无法求解"
        
        # 3. 验证
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.SOLVED:
            is_valid, msg = self.validate(self.result.variables)
            if is_valid:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.VALIDATED
                self.result.confidence = self._calculate_confidence()
            else:
                self.result.error_message = msg
        
        return self.result
    
    def _backtrack(self) -> bool:
        """回溯：放宽上游约束"""
        if not self.upstream_node:
            return False
        
        # 尝试放宽门控阈值 10%
        self._gate_threshold *= 1.1
        logger.warning(f"回溯: 放宽 {self.level.value} 门控阈值至 {self._gate_threshold:.3f}")
        
        # 重新传播上游
        if self.upstream_node.result:
            self.upstream_node._gate_threshold *= 1.05
            return True
        return False
    
    def _calculate_confidence(self) -> float:
        """计算置信度"""
        base_confidence = 0.7
        
        # 材料参数已校准则提高置信度
        if self.level in [ConstraintLevel.V1_MATERIAL, ConstraintLevel.V3_PROCESS]:
            if self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD):
                spec = self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD)
                if spec and spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated:
                    base_confidence += 0.2
        
        return min(base_confidence, 1.0)


class F0_PhysicsNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    F₀ 物理约束层
    
    已知(F):
    - 切割力公式: F = P × L × K (压力×长度×系数)
    - 刀片几何参数
    - 物理定律不可违反
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(ConstraintLevel.F0_PHYSICS, material_db)
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        geometry: DieLineGeometry = input_data.get("geometry")
        material_type: MaterialType = input_data.get("material_type")
        
        if not geometry or not material_type:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message="缺少输入数据"
            )
        
        spec = self.material_db.get_material(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message=f"未知材料类型: {material_type}"
            )
        
        # 计算最小模切压力
        effective_length = geometry.effective_cutting_length() / 10  # cm
        min_pressure = (spec.load_capacity_range.min_val * effective_length * 
                       spec.cutting_force_factor)
        
        # 刀片厚度补偿 [BLOCKED: 使用经验值替代IADD数据]
        blade_compensation = self._get_blade_compensation(geometry.blade_thickness)
        
        return SolveResult(
            level=self.level,
            status=SolveStatus.SOLVED,
            variables={
                "min_cutting_pressure": min_pressure,
                "blade_compensation": blade_compensation,
                "effective_length_cm": effective_length
            },
            constraints={
                "total_length": geometry.total_length,
                "blade_thickness": geometry.blade_thickness,
                "material": material_type.value
            }
        )
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证物理约束"""
        min_pressure = solution.get("min_cutting_pressure", 0)
        if min_pressure <= 0:
            return False, "模切压力必须大于0"
        
        # 物理极限检查
        if min_pressure > 5000:  # 5000N 极限
            return False, f"模切压力 {min_pressure}N 超出设备极限"
        
        return True, ""
    
    def _get_blade_compensation(self, blade_thickness: float) -> float:
        """
        刀片厚度补偿算法
        
        [BLOCKED] 缺乏IADD官方规格数据
        临时方案：使用行业经验值
        - 0.45mm刀片 → 补偿0.15mm
        - 0.71mm刀片 → 补偿0.25mm
        """
        # 线性插值
        if blade_thickness <= 0.45:
            return 0.15
        elif blade_thickness >= 0.71:
            return 0.25
        else:
            return 0.15 + (blade_thickness - 0.45) / (0.71 - 0.45) * 0.10


class V1_MaterialNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    V₁ 材料变量层
    
    未知(V): 材料具体参数需要从经验数据库中选择
    策略：构建参数空间，通过约束传播收窄
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(Constraint

## 第 10 轮
📋 分析:
### 1. 问题要点拆解
- 构建约束传播求解器，实现7级链式收敛：F₀→V₁→F₁→V₂→F₂→V₃→F₃
- 每级F为固定约束，V为待求解变量
- 关联ULDS多层级（L1数学/L2物理/L3化学/L6系统/L8工程）
- 需与Playwright自动验证闭环对接

### 2. 关键概念识别
- **约束传播**：上游F确定后，V的解空间收窄，再固化为下游F
- **链式收敛**：误差逐级传递并累积，需每级设门控阈值
- **材料-结构-工艺耦合**：V₁材料选择直接影响V₂结构设计和V₃工艺参数

### 3. 初步分析结论

**已知(F)梳理：**
| 层级 | 已知固定约束 | 来源 |
|------|-------------|------|
| F₀ | 模切物理定律(切割力=压力×刀线长度)、刀片几何参数 | L2物理 |
| F₁ | 误差不能超过±0.15mm(行业通用公差)、累积误差公式 | L8工程 |
| F₂ | 荷载计算公式(集中力/均布力)、瓦楞纸抗压公式 | L1+L2 |
| F₃ | 质量验收标准(尺寸偏差/压痕深度/切断率) | 行业标准 |
| 代码 | deduction_runner.py推演引擎框架、DB表结构 | 已有基座 |

**未知(V)识别：**
| 变量 | 探索空间 | 不确定度 |
|------|---------|---------|
| V₁ | 纸板/瓦楞/白卡/灰板各自[εmin,εmax]和[Fmin,Fmax] | 高 |
| V₂ | 桥接结构/过桥尺寸/刀线布局的参数化表达 | 中 |
| V₃ | 模切压力、刀片类型选择、压痕线宽深比 | 中 |
| 隐含V | 各级F→V→V→F之间的耦合系数/传递函数 | 高 |

### 4. 双轨推演策略

**对已知——最短路径：**
- 

💻 代码:
# F→V→F 约束传播求解器实现

基于"知与不知"元框架，我将实现7级链式收敛的约束传播求解器。

## 分析结论

**已知(F)**：物理定律、质量标准、已有代码框架
**未知(V)**：材料参数区间、耦合传递函数、工艺参数

**策略**：对已知直接编码，对未知构建自解框架+Playwright验证闭环

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
F→V→F 约束传播求解器 - 刀模设计项目 [p_diepre]
实现7级链式收敛：F₀(物理)→V₁(材料)→F₁(误差范围)→V₂(结构)→F₂(荷载)→V₃(工艺)→F₃(质量)

基于"知与不知"元框架：
- 已知(F): 物理定律、质量标准、已有代码 → 最短路径编码
- 未知(V): 材料参数、耦合系数 → 见路不走，构建自解框架
"""

from __future__ import annotations
import json
import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Optional, Dict, List, Tuple, Any, Callable
from enum import Enum
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
import logging

# 配置日志
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# ============================================================================
# 第一部分：数据结构定义 (已知F的固化)
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintLevel(Enum):
    """约束层级枚举 - ULDS映射"""
    F0_PHYSICS = "F₀物理"      # L2物理：切割力公式、刀片几何
    V1_MATERIAL = "V₁材料"     # L3化学：材料特性参数
    F1_TOLERANCE = "F₁误差"    # L8工程：公差范围、累积误差
    V2_STRUCTURE = "V₂结构"    # L1数学：桥接尺寸、刀线布局
    F2_LOAD = "F₂荷载"         # L2物理：抗压公式、力分布
    V3_PROCESS = "V₃工艺"      # L6系统：模切压力、压痕参数
    F3_QUALITY = "F₃质量"      # L8工程：验收标准


class MaterialType(Enum):
    """材料类型"""
    CARDBOARD = "纸板"
    CORRUGATED = "瓦楞"
    IVORY_BOARD = "白卡"
    GREY_BOARD = "灰板"


class SolveStatus(Enum):
    """求解状态"""
    PENDING = "待求解"
    SOLVED = "已求解"
    VALIDATED = "已验证"
    FAILED = "无解"
    BLOCKED = "阻塞"


@dataclass
class ValueRange:
    """值范围表示 [min, max]"""
    min_val: float
    max_val: float
    unit: str = ""
    is_calibrated: bool = False  # V标记：是否已校准
    
    def contains(self, value: float) -> bool:
        return self.min_val <= value <= self.max_val
    
    def midpoint(self) -> float:
        return (self.min_val + self.max_val) / 2
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "min": self.min_val,
            "max": self.max_val,
            "unit": self.unit,
            "calibrated": self.is_calibrated
        }


@dataclass
class MaterialSpec:
    """材料规格 - V₁变量空间"""
    material_type: MaterialType
    thickness_range: ValueRange      # 厚度范围 mm
    epsilon_range: ValueRange        # 误差范围 mm
    load_capacity_range: ValueRange  # 承载范围 N/cm
    cutting_force_factor: float      # 切割力系数 (V标记: 待校准)
    compression_modulus: float       # 抗压模量 MPa (V标记: 待校准)
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "type": self.material_type.value,
            "thickness": self.thickness_range.to_dict(),
            "epsilon": self.epsilon_range.to_dict(),
            "load_capacity": self.load_capacity_range.to_dict(),
            "cutting_force_factor": self.cutting_force_factor,
            "compression_modulus": self.compression_modulus
        }


@dataclass 
class DieLineGeometry:
    """刀线几何参数"""
    total_length: float      # 总刀线长度 mm
    bridge_count: int        # 过桥数量
    bridge_width: float      # 过桥宽度 mm (标准3-5mm)
    blade_thickness: float   # 刀片厚度 mm [BLOCKED: 缺乏IADD官方数据，使用经验值0.45/0.71]
    blade_height: float      # 刀片高度 mm (标准23.8mm)
    
    def effective_cutting_length(self) -> float:
        """有效切割长度 = 总长度 - 过桥总宽度"""
        return self.total_length - (self.bridge_count * self.bridge_width)


@dataclass
class SolveResult:
    """求解结果"""
    level: ConstraintLevel
    status: SolveStatus
    variables: Dict[str, Any]           # 求解得到的变量
    constraints: Dict[str, Any]         # 固化的约束
    confidence: float = 0.0             # 置信度 0-1
    error_message: str = ""
    blocked_reason: str = ""


# ============================================================================
# 第二部分：材料经验数据库 (V₁未知→构建自解框架)
# ============================================================================

class MaterialDatabase:
    """
    材料特性数据库
    
    策略：见路不走 - 不依赖IADD官方数据(已阻塞)
    采用反向工程法：从已有刀模图成品反推参数区间
    所有值标记为V(待校准)，通过Playwright验证闭环逐步固化为F
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self._materials: Dict[MaterialType, MaterialSpec] = {}
        self._calibration_history: List[Dict] = []
        self._initialize_empirical_data()
    
    def _initialize_empirical_data(self):
        """初始化经验数据 - 基于行业通用值"""
        
        # 纸板：常见包装材料
        self._materials[MaterialType.CARDBOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CARDBOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.3, 1.5, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.08, 0.20, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(50, 200, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.0,  # 基准值
            compression_modulus=15.0   # 待校准
        )
        
        # 瓦楞纸：缓冲包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.CORRUGATED] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CORRUGATED,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(2.0, 8.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.15, 0.35, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(30, 120, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=0.7,
            compression_modulus=8.0
        )
        
        # 白卡纸：精品包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.2, 0.8, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.05, 0.15, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(80, 300, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.3,
            compression_modulus=25.0
        )
        
        # 灰板：精装书/礼盒
        self._materials[MaterialType.GREY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.GREY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(1.0, 3.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.20, 0.50, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(100, 400, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.5,
            compression_modulus=35.0
        )
        
        logger.info(f"材料数据库初始化完成: {len(self._materials)}种材料 (全部标记为待校准V)")
    
    def get_material(self, material_type: MaterialType) -> Optional[MaterialSpec]:
        return self._materials.get(material_type)
    
    def calibrate_from_validation(self, material_type: MaterialType, 
                                   validated_params: Dict[str, float],
                                   test_result: bool) -> bool:
        """
        从Playwright验证结果反校准参数
        V→F转化：验证通过后固化为已知
        """
        spec = self._materials.get(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return False
        
        # 记录校准历史
        calibration_record = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "material": material_type.value,
            "params": validated_params,
            "result": "PASS" if test_result else "FAIL"
        }
        self._calibration_history.append(calibration_record)
        
        if test_result:
            # 验证通过，收窄参数区间
            if "epsilon" in validated_params:
                eps = validated_params["epsilon"]
                # 贝叶斯更新：收窄区间
                spec.epsilon_range.min_val = max(spec.epsilon_range.min_val, eps * 0.8)
                spec.epsilon_range.max_val = min(spec.epsilon_range.max_val, eps * 1.2)
                spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            if "load" in validated_params:
                load = validated_params["load"]
                spec.load_capacity_range.min_val = max(spec.load_capacity_range.min_val, load * 0.9)
                spec.load_capacity_range.max_val = min(spec.load_capacity_range.max_val, load * 1.1)
                spec.load_capacity_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            logger.info(f"材料 {material_type.value} 参数校准完成")
        
        return True
    
    def export_calibration_report(self) -> Dict:
        """导出校准报告"""
        return {
            "materials": {k.value: v.to_dict() for k, v in self._materials.items()},
            "calibration_history": self._calibration_history[-10:],  # 最近10条
            "unresolved_v_count": sum(1 for v in self._materials.values() 
                                     if not v.epsilon_range.is_calibrated)
        }


# ============================================================================
# 第三部分：约束节点与链式传播引擎
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintNode:
    """
    约束节点 - F→V→F链式收敛的基本单元
    
    每个节点包含：
    - F: 固定约束（来自上游或物理定律）
    - V: 待求解变量
    - solve(): 求解V
    - validate(): 验证解是否满足约束
    """
    
    def __init__(self, level: ConstraintLevel, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        self.level = level
        self.material_db = material_db
        self.upstream_node: Optional[ConstraintNode] = None
        self.result: Optional[SolveResult] = None
        self._gate_threshold = 0.15  # 门控阈值 mm
    
    def set_upstream(self, node: ConstraintNode):
        """设置上游节点"""
        self.upstream_node = node
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """求解当前层级的V变量"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证解是否满足约束"""
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def propagate(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        """
        链式传播：求解→验证→返回结果
        若无解，触发回溯或标记阻塞
        """
        # 1. 求解
        self.result = self.solve(input_data)
        
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.FAILED:
            # 2. 无解时尝试回溯
            if self.upstream_node and self._backtrack():
                # 回溯成功，重新求解
                self.result = self.solve(input_data)
            else:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.BLOCKED
                self.result.blocked_reason = "上游约束过紧，无法求解"
        
        # 3. 验证
        if self.result.status == SolveStatus.SOLVED:
            is_valid, msg = self.validate(self.result.variables)
            if is_valid:
                self.result.status = SolveStatus.VALIDATED
                self.result.confidence = self._calculate_confidence()
            else:
                self.result.error_message = msg
        
        return self.result
    
    def _backtrack(self) -> bool:
        """回溯：放宽上游约束"""
        if not self.upstream_node:
            return False
        
        # 尝试放宽门控阈值 10%
        self._gate_threshold *= 1.1
        logger.warning(f"回溯: 放宽 {self.level.value} 门控阈值至 {self._gate_threshold:.3f}")
        
        # 重新传播上游
        if self.upstream_node.result:
            self.upstream_node._gate_threshold *= 1.05
            return True
        return False
    
    def _calculate_confidence(self) -> float:
        """计算置信度"""
        base_confidence = 0.7
        
        # 材料参数已校准则提高置信度
        if self.level in [ConstraintLevel.V1_MATERIAL, ConstraintLevel.V3_PROCESS]:
            if self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD):
                spec = self.material_db.get_material(MaterialType.CARDBOARD)
                if spec and spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated:
                    base_confidence += 0.2
        
        return min(base_confidence, 1.0)


class F0_PhysicsNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    F₀ 物理约束层
    
    已知(F):
    - 切割力公式: F = P × L × K (压力×长度×系数)
    - 刀片几何参数
    - 物理定律不可违反
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(ConstraintLevel.F0_PHYSICS, material_db)
    
    def solve(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> SolveResult:
        geometry: DieLineGeometry = input_data.get("geometry")
        material_type: MaterialType = input_data.get("material_type")
        
        if not geometry or not material_type:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message="缺少输入数据"
            )
        
        spec = self.material_db.get_material(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return SolveResult(
                level=self.level,
                status=SolveStatus.FAILED,
                variables={},
                constraints={},
                error_message=f"未知材料类型: {material_type}"
            )
        
        # 计算最小模切压力
        effective_length = geometry.effective_cutting_length() / 10  # cm
        min_pressure = (spec.load_capacity_range.min_val * effective_length * 
                       spec.cutting_force_factor)
        
        # 刀片厚度补偿 [BLOCKED: 使用经验值替代IADD数据]
        blade_compensation = self._get_blade_compensation(geometry.blade_thickness)
        
        return SolveResult(
            level=self.level,
            status=SolveStatus.SOLVED,
            variables={
                "min_cutting_pressure": min_pressure,
                "blade_compensation": blade_compensation,
                "effective_length_cm": effective_length
            },
            constraints={
                "total_length": geometry.total_length,
                "blade_thickness": geometry.blade_thickness,
                "material": material_type.value
            }
        )
    
    def validate(self, solution: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """验证物理约束"""
        min_pressure = solution.get("min_cutting_pressure", 0)
        if min_pressure <= 0:
            return False, "模切压力必须大于0"
        
        # 物理极限检查
        if min_pressure > 5000:  # 5000N 极限
            return False, f"模切压力 {min_pressure}N 超出设备极限"
        
        return True, ""
    
    def _get_blade_compensation(self, blade_thickness: float) -> float:
        """
        刀片厚度补偿算法
        
        [BLOCKED] 缺乏IADD官方规格数据
        临时方案：使用行业经验值
        - 0.45mm刀片 → 补偿0.15mm
        - 0.71mm刀片 → 补偿0.25mm
        """
        # 线性插值
        if blade_thickness <= 0.45:
            return 0.15
        elif blade_thickness >= 0.71:
            return 0.25
        else:
            return 0.15 + (blade_thickness - 0.45) / (0.71 - 0.45) * 0.10


class V1_MaterialNode(ConstraintNode):
    """
    V₁ 材料变量层
    
    未知(V): 材料具体参数需要从经验数据库中选择
    策略：构建参数空间，通过约束传播收窄
    """
    
    def __init__(self, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        super().__init__(Constraint

🛡️ 风险提示:
- [CD03] 内存泄漏: 循环引用/未释放资源/无限增长缓存
- [CD07] SQL注入/命令注入: 字符串拼接构建查询/命令

## 第 11 轮
📋 分析:
### 1. 问题要点拆解
- 构建约束传播求解器，实现7级链式收敛：F₀→V₁→F₁→V₂→F₂→V₃→F₃
- 每级F为固定约束，V为待求解变量
- 关联ULDS多层级（L1数学/L2物理/L3化学/L6系统/L8工程）
- 需与Playwright自动验证闭环对接

### 2. 关键概念识别
- **约束传播**：上游F确定后，V的解空间收窄，再固化为下游F
- **链式收敛**：误差逐级传递并累积，需每级设门控阈值
- **材料-结构-工艺耦合**：V₁材料选择直接影响V₂结构设计和V₃工艺参数

### 3. 初步分析结论

**已知(F)梳理：**
| 层级 | 已知固定约束 | 来源 |
|------|-------------|------|
| F₀ | 模切物理定律(切割力=压力×刀线长度)、刀片几何参数 | L2物理 |
| F₁ | 误差不能超过±0.15mm(行业通用公差)、累积误差公式 | L8工程 |
| F₂ | 荷载计算公式(集中力/均布力)、瓦楞纸抗压公式 | L1+L2 |
| F₃ | 质量验收标准(尺寸偏差/压痕深度/切断率) | 行业标准 |
| 代码 | deduction_runner.py推演引擎框架、DB表结构 | 已有基座 |

**未知(V)识别：**
| 变量 | 探索空间 | 不确定度 |
|------|---------|---------|
| V₁ | 纸板/瓦楞/白卡/灰板各自[εmin,εmax]和[Fmin,Fmax] | 高 |
| V₂ | 桥接结构/过桥尺寸/刀线布局的参数化表达 | 中 |
| V₃ | 模切压力、刀片类型选择、压痕线宽深比 | 中 |
| 隐含V | 各级F→V→V→F之间的耦合系数/传递函数 | 高 |

### 4. 双轨推演策略

**对已知——最短路径：**
- 

💻 代码:
# F→V→F 约束传播求解器实现

基于"知与不知"元框架，我将实现7级链式收敛的约束传播求解器。

## 分析结论

**已知(F)**：物理定律、质量标准、已有代码框架
**未知(V)**：材料参数区间、耦合传递函数、工艺参数

**策略**：对已知直接编码，对未知构建自解框架+Playwright验证闭环

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
F→V→F 约束传播求解器 - 刀模设计项目 [p_diepre]
实现7级链式收敛：F₀(物理)→V₁(材料)→F₁(误差范围)→V₂(结构)→F₂(荷载)→V₃(工艺)→F₃(质量)

基于"知与不知"元框架：
- 已知(F): 物理定律、质量标准、已有代码 → 最短路径编码
- 未知(V): 材料参数、耦合系数 → 见路不走，构建自解框架
"""

from __future__ import annotations
import json
import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Optional, Dict, List, Tuple, Any, Callable
from enum import Enum
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
import logging

# 配置日志
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# ============================================================================
# 第一部分：数据结构定义 (已知F的固化)
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintLevel(Enum):
    """约束层级枚举 - ULDS映射"""
    F0_PHYSICS = "F₀物理"      # L2物理：切割力公式、刀片几何
    V1_MATERIAL = "V₁材料"     # L3化学：材料特性参数
    F1_TOLERANCE = "F₁误差"    # L8工程：公差范围、累积误差
    V2_STRUCTURE = "V₂结构"    # L1数学：桥接尺寸、刀线布局
    F2_LOAD = "F₂荷载"         # L2物理：抗压公式、力分布
    V3_PROCESS = "V₃工艺"      # L6系统：模切压力、压痕参数
    F3_QUALITY = "F₃质量"      # L8工程：验收标准


class MaterialType(Enum):
    """材料类型"""
    CARDBOARD = "纸板"
    CORRUGATED = "瓦楞"
    IVORY_BOARD = "白卡"
    GREY_BOARD = "灰板"


class SolveStatus(Enum):
    """求解状态"""
    PENDING = "待求解"
    SOLVED = "已求解"
    VALIDATED = "已验证"
    FAILED = "无解"
    BLOCKED = "阻塞"


@dataclass
class ValueRange:
    """值范围表示 [min, max]"""
    min_val: float
    max_val: float
    unit: str = ""
    is_calibrated: bool = False  # V标记：是否已校准
    
    def contains(self, value: float) -> bool:
        return self.min_val <= value <= self.max_val
    
    def midpoint(self) -> float:
        return (self.min_val + self.max_val) / 2
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "min": self.min_val,
            "max": self.max_val,
            "unit": self.unit,
            "calibrated": self.is_calibrated
        }


@dataclass
class MaterialSpec:
    """材料规格 - V₁变量空间"""
    material_type: MaterialType
    thickness_range: ValueRange      # 厚度范围 mm
    epsilon_range: ValueRange        # 误差范围 mm
    load_capacity_range: ValueRange  # 承载范围 N/cm
    cutting_force_factor: float      # 切割力系数 (V标记: 待校准)
    compression_modulus: float       # 抗压模量 MPa (V标记: 待校准)
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "type": self.material_type.value,
            "thickness": self.thickness_range.to_dict(),
            "epsilon": self.epsilon_range.to_dict(),
            "load_capacity": self.load_capacity_range.to_dict(),
            "cutting_force_factor": self.cutting_force_factor,
            "compression_modulus": self.compression_modulus
        }


@dataclass 
class DieLineGeometry:
    """刀线几何参数"""
    total_length: float      # 总刀线长度 mm
    bridge_count: int        # 过桥数量
    bridge_width: float      # 过桥宽度 mm (标准3-5mm)
    blade_thickness: float   # 刀片厚度 mm [BLOCKED: 缺乏IADD官方数据，使用经验值0.45/0.71]
    blade_height: float      # 刀片高度 mm (标准23.8mm)
    
    def effective_cutting_length(self) -> float:
        """有效切割长度 = 总长度 - 过桥总宽度"""
        return self.total_length - (self.bridge_count * self.bridge_width)


@dataclass
class SolveResult:
    """求解结果"""
    level: ConstraintLevel
    status: SolveStatus
    variables: Dict[str, Any]           # 求解得到的变量
    constraints: Dict[str, Any]         # 固化的约束
    confidence: float = 0.0             # 置信度 0-1
    error_message: str = ""
    blocked_reason: str = ""


# ============================================================================
# 第二部分：材料经验数据库 (V₁未知→构建自解框架)
# ============================================================================

class MaterialDatabase:
    """
    材料特性数据库
    
    策略：见路不走 - 不依赖IADD官方数据(已阻塞)
    采用反向工程法：从已有刀模图成品反推参数区间
    所有值标记为V(待校准)，通过Playwright验证闭环逐步固化为F
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self._materials: Dict[MaterialType, MaterialSpec] = {}
        self._calibration_history: List[Dict] = []
        self._initialize_empirical_data()
    
    def _initialize_empirical_data(self):
        """初始化经验数据 - 基于行业通用值"""
        
        # 纸板：常见包装材料
        self._materials[MaterialType.CARDBOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CARDBOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.3, 1.5, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.08, 0.20, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(50, 200, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.0,  # 基准值
            compression_modulus=15.0   # 待校准
        )
        
        # 瓦楞纸：缓冲包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.CORRUGATED] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.CORRUGATED,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(2.0, 8.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.15, 0.35, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(30, 120, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=0.7,
            compression_modulus=8.0
        )
        
        # 白卡纸：精品包装
        self._materials[MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.IVORY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(0.2, 0.8, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.05, 0.15, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(80, 300, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.3,
            compression_modulus=25.0
        )
        
        # 灰板：精装书/礼盒
        self._materials[MaterialType.GREY_BOARD] = MaterialSpec(
            material_type=MaterialType.GREY_BOARD,
            thickness_range=ValueRange(1.0, 3.0, "mm"),
            epsilon_range=ValueRange(0.20, 0.50, "mm", is_calibrated=False),
            load_capacity_range=ValueRange(100, 400, "N/cm", is_calibrated=False),
            cutting_force_factor=1.5,
            compression_modulus=35.0
        )
        
        logger.info(f"材料数据库初始化完成: {len(self._materials)}种材料 (全部标记为待校准V)")
    
    def get_material(self, material_type: MaterialType) -> Optional[MaterialSpec]:
        return self._materials.get(material_type)
    
    def calibrate_from_validation(self, material_type: MaterialType, 
                                   validated_params: Dict[str, float],
                                   test_result: bool) -> bool:
        """
        从Playwright验证结果反校准参数
        V→F转化：验证通过后固化为已知
        """
        spec = self._materials.get(material_type)
        if not spec:
            return False
        
        # 记录校准历史
        calibration_record = {
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "material": material_type.value,
            "params": validated_params,
            "result": "PASS" if test_result else "FAIL"
        }
        self._calibration_history.append(calibration_record)
        
        if test_result:
            # 验证通过，收窄参数区间
            if "epsilon" in validated_params:
                eps = validated_params["epsilon"]
                # 贝叶斯更新：收窄区间
                spec.epsilon_range.min_val = max(spec.epsilon_range.min_val, eps * 0.8)
                spec.epsilon_range.max_val = min(spec.epsilon_range.max_val, eps * 1.2)
                spec.epsilon_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            if "load" in validated_params:
                load = validated_params["load"]
                spec.load_capacity_range.min_val = max(spec.load_capacity_range.min_val, load * 0.9)
                spec.load_capacity_range.max_val = min(spec.load_capacity_range.max_val, load * 1.1)
                spec.load_capacity_range.is_calibrated = True
            
            logger.info(f"材料 {material_type.value} 参数校准完成")
        
        return True
    
    def export_calibration_report(self) -> Dict:
        """导出校准报告"""
        return {
            "materials": {k.value: v.to_dict() for k, v in self._materials.items()},
            "calibration_history": self._calibration_history[-10:],  # 最近10条
            "unresolved_v_count": sum(1 for v in self._materials.values() 
                                     if not v.epsilon_range.is_calibrated)
        }


# ============================================================================
# 第三部分：约束节点与链式传播引擎
# ============================================================================

class ConstraintNode:
    """
    约束节点 - F→V→F链式收敛的基本单元
    
    每个节点包含：
    - F: 固定约束（来自上游或物理定律）
    - V: 待求解变量
    - solve(): 求解V
    - validate(): 验证解是否满足约束
    """
    
    def __init__(self, level: ConstraintLevel, material_db: MaterialDatabase):
        self.level = level
        self.material_db = material_db
        self.upstream_node: Optional[ConstraintNode] = None
        self.result: Optional[SolveResult] = None
        self._gate_threshold = 0.15  # 门控阈值 mm
    
    def set_upstream(self, node: ConstraintNode):
